a = [10  8 -3 1;2 10 1 -4 ;3 -4 10 1;2 2 -3 10];
b = [16;9;10;11];
y = [a,b];
n = size(a,1);
l = eye(n)
for i = 1:n-1
    for j = i+1:n
        y(j,:) = y(j,:) - y(j,:)*y(j,i)/y(i,i);
    end
end
u = y(:,1:n)
b = y(:,1+n)
y = inv(l)*b;
x = inv(u)*y;
disp(x)

clear all
A=[4.63,-1.21,3.22;-3.07,5.48,2.11;1.26,3.11,4.57];
B=[2.22,-3.17,5.11];
tol=0.001;
N=100
n=length(B);
x0=zeros(n,1);
x=zeros(n,1);
k=1;
while(k<=N)
    for i=1:n
      sum1=0;
      for j=1:i-1
          sum1=sum1+A(i,j)*x(j)
      end
      sum2=0;
      for j=i+1:n
          sum2=sum2+A(i,j)*x0(j)
      end
      x(i)=(B(i)-sum1-sum2)/A(i,i)
    end
    if(abs(x-x0)<tol)
        break;
    else
        x0=x;
        k=k+1;
    end

-- Uncomment the following library declaration if instantiating
-- any Xilinx primitives in this code.
--library UNISIM;
--use UNISIM.VComponents.all;

entity decoder3to8 is
    Port ( i : in  STD_LOGIC_VECTOR (2 downto 0);
           y : out  STD_LOGIC_VECTOR (7 downto 0));
end decoder3to8;

architecture Behavioral of decoder3to8 is
signal sb2, sb1, sb0: std_logic;

begin

sb2<= not i(2);
sb1<= not i(1);
sb0<= not i(0);

y(0)<= (sb2 AND sb1 AND sb0);
y(1)<= (sb2 AND sb1 AND i(0));
y(2)<= (sb2 AND i(1) AND sb0);
y(3)<= (sb2 AND i(1) AND i(0));
y(4)<= (i(2) AND sb1 AND sb0);
y(5)<= (i(2) AND sb1 AND i(0));
y(6)<= (i(2) AND i(1) AND sb0);
y(7)<= (i(2) AND i(1) AND i(0));











end Behavioral;

23/02/2023, 19:42 - Aditya EC7: clc
clear all
n = -10:10;
unitstep1 = n>=0;
unitstep2 = n>=6;
x = unitstep1 - unitstep2;
subplot(2,2,1)
stem(n, x)
xlabel('time');
ylabel('Amplitude');
title('Input function')
legend('Aditya 102106179')

h = unitstep1 - unitstep2;
subplot(2,2,2)
stem(n, h)
xlabel('time');
ylabel('Amplitude');
title('Impulse function')

a = length(x);
b = length(h);
N = a+b-1;

X = [x, zeros(1,N-a)];
H = [h, zeros(1,N-b)];

for n = 1:N
    y(n) = 0;
    for k = 1:a
        
        if(k <= n)
            y(n) = y(n) + X(k)*H(n-k+1);
        end
    end
end
n1 = -20:20
subplot(2,2,3)
stem(n1, y)
xlabel('time');
ylabel('Amplitude');
title('Convolution without inbuilt function')

z = conv(x,h)
subplot(2,2,4)
stem(n1,z)
xlabel('time');
ylabel('Amplitude');
title('Convolution with inbuilt function')
